(ENG)

Extinction Rebellion decided to end the fourth Storm Warning demonstration on Porkkalankatu and Mechelininkatu to protect protesters from police violence.

The police started making arrests immediately after the protest started and announced they would use force against peaceful protesters if they stepped onto the roadway. The police did not instruct the protesters to move to another location nor gave specific dispersal orders before starting to use force.

Protesters witnessed several instances of excessive force by the police: officers hit a protester's head with a banner stick, strangled a legal observer, dragged protesters across the asphalt by a single limb, and threw and knocked over protesters.

The goal of Extinction Rebellion protests is not to oppose the police but to create political pressure that gains critical climate and environmental issues broader public awareness. The purpose of our action is to get decision-makers to act in accordance with the demands of the climate and environmental emergency.

The police's role is to ensure the safety of protesters, but targeting peaceful demonstrators with force to fulfill this statutory duty is unnecessary.

Read our full press release: elokapina.fi üì¢
